BSTAN SRUŃ RGYA MISHO
VOLUME 1



Bstan srung
Dam can bstan srung rgya mtsho'i ram par thar pa cha shas
tsam brjod pa sngon med legs bshad.
Manuscript ledger in the possession of Khri-byang Rin-po-che.
(another copy is reported to be in Bhutan)
pp. 153 (i. e. 306 +)
Author: Sle-lung Rje-drung Bzhad-pa'i-rdo-rje.
Written in 1734.

Śiva
du Izhag go/ de nas hūm mdzad kyis bcom 1dan 'das la ji
Itar bgyi zhus pas/ om badzra a ka ma hoh zhes gsungs
pas/ hūm mdzad kyis/ u ma gan rkyal du bsgyel te zhabs
g.yas pas mnan/ lha chen kha sbub tu bsgyel te zhabs g.yon
pas mnan/ snying po gsung ma thag tu lha chen la byin
babs te/ rang gi phyag stong gis rang la dbang med du
'tshog par mdzad do/
/der dkyil 'khor gyi phyi rol na gnas pa'i dbang phyug
gi 'khor srid gsum gyi bdag po mnams kyis ngrin gcig tu
bdag cag gi dbang po ni bdag nyid chen po rdo rje hūm
mdzad kyis btul lo/ zhes pa'i sgra sa g.yo ba tsam du
bsgrags so/ der mam snang gis byams pa'i snying po gsungs
pa lha chen la byin phebs pas sdug bsngal zhi ste/ rang
gi lus hüm mdzad la gdan du phul nas log phyogs kyi 'jig
rten gyi khams ganggā'i klung sum cu so gnyis kyi bye ma
snyed 'das pa na thal bas khebs pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten
gyi khams su de bzhin gshegs pa thal ba'i dbang po'i dbyangs

es mal
/dur khrod gnas su 'dul bar mdzad pas ni/
Śiva
/gdul bya'i ming ni 'dul byed la grags 'gyur/
/las rgyal mchog gi 'phrin las bstan pa'o/ /zhes mal
'byor ma snying po'i rgyud las gsungs so zhes lung du drangs
so/ /zhes shāk thub 'dzam gling du byon nas drag po dbang phyug
chen po btul bar gsungs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir ma zad/
'dzam bu'i gling bye ba phrag brgya sogs zhing rdul gyi
grangs dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dbang phyug
'dul ba'i bkod pa sna tshogs pa bstan pas don dam par dus
snga phyi dang btul tshul gyi bkod pa sogs la mtha' cig tu
'jog par mi nus te/ mngon briod 'grel par/
ji skad du/ de nas longs spyod rdzogs pa'i skus gdul bya.
sna tshogs pa la gzigs pas 'dul byed kyi 'khor lo dgongs
pa sna tshogs pa kho dog dang dbyibs tha dad pa'i kun
rdzob kyi dam tshig chen pos rnam par rol cing sprul
pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i yul de la amigs pa'i ting
nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ snod kyi 'jig rten ma
lus shing shing bcud kyi sems lus pa med pa'i sems can
byang chub kyi snying po can gyi chos kyi dbyings kyi
snang ba kun tu gang bar gzigs nas gdul bya de'i don
du longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i rang gi ba spu'i bu
ga nas gling bzhi sa bye ba phrag brgyar dal gyi 'khor
lo sna tshogs pa spros te gdul bya sna tshogs pa 'dul
ba'i thabs kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs pa'i thabs kyis
nam mkha'i khams gang bar gdul bya snod dang ldan pa
mnams kyi lha'i mig dang ma ba la snang bar gyur ro/
/'dzam bu'i gling yon tan rgyal mtshan 'dir bcom idan

dong du bcug nas rang gi lhas dmod pas: sangs rgyas 'khor bcas
rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkha' la gshegs pas: de'i tshe rgyal po
dga' rab dbang phyug btsun mo padma'i 'phreng ba sogs kyis
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la gnod pa'i smon lam log par btab:
sangs rgyas kyi 'khor de'i nang nas dgra bcom zhi ba 'od dang:
de bzhin du smon lam 'grub pa mang pos 'di ltar btab bo:
bda g cag dge slong pho mo mnams :
tshangs spyod bsod nams sngags mthu yis:
skye ba 'di nas gnyis 'das nas:
srid pa gsum na dbang che ba:
gnod sbyin gdug pa srin po'i rigs:
sha za khrag 'thung srog gi bdag:
las kyi gshin rjer smon lam btab:
smon lam bden pa'i byin brlabs kyis:
sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung bar shog: ces rang gi ston
pa'i spyan sngar btab pas: de'i bden pas ri rab ri yi rtse
mo na lha chen dbang phyug chen po dang: btsun mo u ma de wi
gnyis la bu brgyad skyes pas lha chen po brgyad du byung: de
rjes la dpal chen po he ru kas bdud sde rams 'dul ba'i ched
du lha mo u ma de wī gnyis la dgyes pa'i gad mo bcu gnyis
kyis sbyor ba byas pas: de la rdo rje srin po rab tu khros pas
dpal ye shes kyi mgon po bya rog mtshan can phyag bzhi pa 'khrungs
so:
de Itar lha brgyad: dpal mgon dang dgu yi rkan mar du:
mi rta'i sha: rgun 'brum: la phug: sgog pa: bu ram: chang: g.yag



Mgon-po
Ma-ning
lug ra gsum gyi sha khrag rams byin nas: srid pa gsum gyi
mnga' bdag sangs rgyas bstan pa skyong ba'i lung mar smon lam
btab bo:
de nas rdo rje srin po des khams gsum dbang du bsdus:
bdud kyi blon po bzhi bsgral nas gsang ba'i yum bzhi la sbyor
bas: gsang ba'i bu bzhi skyes te: bya rog gdong: 'bar ma bya
rog: seng gdong: ra hu la dang bzhi skyes so:
de'i tshe de'i dus su: bdud dga' rab abang phyug yid ma
dga' nas 'khrugs te: "jig rten gyi khams thams cad goyo ba'i
'khrul 'khor la bzhugs te: lha ma yin gyi dmag bye ba dung
phyug mang po bsdus te nam mkha' la thog dang: me dang: 'brug
dang: drag po'i cho 'phrul chen po bcu drug gis g.yos te: srin
yul du gnas boas nas ljig rten khams kyi sems can thams cad
la gnod pa'i las kyis bsad cing bzas nas stongs la thugs:
sangs rgyas bstan pa gar yod du dgrar ltas nas brlag: sum cu
rtsa gsum gyi lha mnams kyang brlag nas gnod pa'i tshe: lha'i
dbang po brgya byin gyis 'jig rten 'dir bdud kyi dmag 'dul
yod pa su yod snyam nas: lha yi mig gis bltas pas: lha chen
gyi abu bya rog gi ming de gdug cing drag rtsal Idan pas des
thul bar mthong nas: lha min g.yul ngo bzlog phyir: tshangs
pa'i bu mo yid 'ongs ma dpal 'bar tsandi ka dang: bzhin ndzes
rgyan bzang: lha mo brgyad dang bcas pas lus phul nas spyan
'dren btang bas: rdo rje srin po des kyang sngon gyi skye gnas
dran nas dus la babs par dgongs te sum cu rtsa gsum du byon:
de'i tshe rdo rje srin po rab tu khros pa las: bdud 'dul
ba'i thabs bstan pas: bdud dga' rab dbang phyug la zhal bzhi
yod pas: de la bdud kyi sku bzhi byung bas: de 'dul ba la gsang
ba'i lha mo bzhi sprul: bdud kyi spyan la dug bzhi yod pas:
de 'dul ba la phyag bzhi nas 'phrin las kyi rgyal po bzhi
sprul: de bzhin du dpal mgon gyi skye mched drug las mkha' 'gro
ma drug sprul: ram shes tshogs brgyad las bka' sdod (p. 31a)

brgyad sprul: rig pa'i yan lag bcu las phyogs skyong bcu: dbang Mgon-po
Ma-ning

de nas srin po'i gzugs can des chos bzang lha'i bdun sar

byung/ sku gsung thugs kyi sprul pa bya seng rā hu 'bar ma

sa bdag gi dmag bsdus: bgegs rgyal byi na ya kas byang bgegs

Bsil-ba'i-
tshal
rigs stong phrag brgyad cu'i dmag bsdus: Ito 'phye nag po mig
dgus log min sa bdag rgyal po'i dmag bsdus: rtsa lung nag po
dur 'gyed kyis gnod sbyin ser nag bcas bsdus: bdud rgyal bye ba
dgu ring gis ma mo khram gyi bdag po'i dmag bsdus: bdud dga'
rab dbang phyug gis baud dang srin po'i dmag mams bsdus nas:
thams cad ri rab ri yi rtse mor mun pa'i sprin dang gnag po'i
'od: mtshon cha sna tshogs kyi char dang: ri phran 'phen cing
thog ser glog dang 'brug sgra: me chu rlung gis bskal pa dang:
nad dang dug gi sprin nag 'khrigs shing bdud kyi bu mo bslu
brid mkhan dang bcas drag po'i bso yis btab nas rtsod pa la
chas so:-
de nas lha dbang brgya byin gyis lha dmag bye ba dung
phyur dang bcas pa bsil ba'i tshal du chas: rdo rje srin pos
sprul pa dung phyug mang po dang bcas nas dga' ba'i tshal du
chas: pho bo lha chen gyis lha dmag bye ba dung phyur dang
bcas byang gser gyi brag rtsar chas nas hūn phat kyi sgra yis
srid gsum 'gul lo:
de nas bdud tshogs dmag dpung bcas pa rtsub 'gyur lha yi
mdun par rgol ba la phyin pas: de'i tshe dpal ye shes kyi mgon
pos gri gug dang: ral gri las tshogs kyi bdag po sogs lha
dmag bye ba dung phyur sprul: 'jigs pa'i gar stabs sum cu las
sde dpon sum cu sogs lha dmag bye ba dung phyur sprul nas lha
min zhe sdang gi g.yul ngo bzlog: bdud dga' rab dbang phyug
bsad nas mkhal na snying dang nang khrel bton nas lus po cha
brgyad du bgos (p. 31b) te: dur khrod brgyad du byin gyis brlabs:
kho yi gna, s srin po langka pu ri'i gnas su srin po'i grong
khyer bdun 'bum brlag: g.yas pa gri gug gis srin po'i mgo bcad:
nang khrol phyungs snying khrag 'thung: lha min bu mo glog ma
sprin gyi mgo bcad nas 'phreng ba byas: rgyal po'i g.yag lug
ra dang: rta nag (srin pos) dre'u (bdud kyi) bya nag/ dom nag/
khyi spyang: klu yi sirui dang rlung nag: ma mo'i dar nag re

Mgon-po
Ma-ning
nag thams cad 'phrogs nas blangs: srid gsum bye ba phrag
brgya dbang du bsdus nas rgyal drag pos hūm hūm phat phat
kyi sgra sgrogs pas: kha nas me 'bar rgya mtsho skem zhing
mgams pa'i nga ros 'ur 'ur chems chem shigs shig tu sprin
nag 'khrigs shing/ thog dang ser ba 'brug rnams bsgrags lha
min bdud kyi dmag dpon brgyad ni phu bo bka' sdod lha chen
brgyad kyis bsad nas ngo bcad thod pa khrag bkang gsol zhing:
snying ni gtso bo la bstab: bdud kyi dmag dpon brgyad ni byang
phyogs gnod sbyin brgyad kyis btul: u dhi ha la sogs lha min
gyi blon po chen po brgyad ni nub phyogs klu chen po brgyad
kyis beings: 'gugs byed ma sogs bdud kyi dmag khrom bdag chen
po brgyad ni: lho phyogs kyi gshin rje dang gza' brgyad kyis
bsgral: lha min gyi bdud dmag thans cad brlag par byas nas

nya nyi shu las byed du bskol: dbang phyug nyi shu rtsa brgyad

'bum ni bran dang bka' nyan la bskos: sha za bye ba'i tshogs
ni bka'i bya ra mngag gzhug la bskos nas lha thams cad bde

padma dbang gis dam la btags shing:

Ma-ning
'bum sngon la rgyug: glang chen smyon pa 'bum phyi nas 'breng
gser gyi seng ge 'bum zur nas 'gying: lcags kyi bya khra 'bum

rlog/ lcags kyi phag rgod 'bum gyis ngur sgra sgrogs pa sogs/

yang gsungs so/

'das kyi dregs pa 'dul ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs

pas/ skad cig nyid la sprul pa'i ngon po ma hā kā la phyag

byed srog gi spu gri'i rgyud gsungs par bshad/ mam thos sras
kyis bskul ma mdzad de/ mgon po 'di nyid ma 'ongs pa na byang
shar thal ba'i 'jig rten du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thal ba'i
dbang po zhes bya bar sangs rgya bar gsungs te/ rgyud de'i
le'u nyer gnyis pa las/
ngo bo bde mchog dpa' bo yi/
/ye shes sku de rdo rje 'dzin/
de las sprul pa dpal 'bar ba/
khrag 'thung legs ldan nag po che/
/sku bzhi mthar phyin rdo rje 'chang/
/chos sku longs sku sprul pa'i sku/
/bde ba chen po'i sku dang bzhi/
Adam pa chos skyong srung ma stel
/ma 'ongs dus mtha'i bskal pa las/
/byang shar thal ba'i 'jig rten du/
/thal ba'i dbang por sangs rgyas nas/



Bstan srung
68
Mgon-po
Ma-ning
/bstan pa mi nub rgyas par byed/ /ces gsungs pas mgon po
'di nyid lha chen dpal 'bar ram ma ning nag po yin par bstan
cing/ de nyid dbang phyug chen po yin par grub ste/ de bzhin
gshegs pa thal ba'i dbang po ni dbang phyug sangs rgyas pa'i
sangs rgyas yin par gsungs so/
/rgyud sde mams su dbang phyug sa 'og tu de bzhin gshegs
pa thal ba'i dbang por sangs rgyas zin par bshad pa dang/ 'dir
ma 'ongs pa na sangs rgyas 'gyur gsungs pa dang/ ma ning dang
mgon po 'di la lar yab sras dang/ la lar sku dngos rang yin
par gsungs pa dang/ yum amar mo rtsa 'jib ma'an tsandi ka bdud
santanperdang kyi lag nas 'phrogs te yum du bzhes par gsungs
pa dang/ sring mo tsa muntri nyid tsandi kar bshad pa dang/
mgon po 'di'i yum gyi bstod pa las/
nam mkha'i gos can khyod la bstod/ /ces pa dang/
lha mo dus mtshan re ma ti/
e ka dza ti ral goig ma/
/phyag bzhi ma la mdzes ma ste/ /zhes nam mkha'i gos can
ma dang/ dus mtshan lha mo 'od chen "bar ma dang/ e ka dza ţi
la sogs yin par gsungs pa ni gdul bya so so'i snang tshul la
Itos nas bkod pa tha dad du ma dus gcig tu byung ba yin pas.
'gal ba mi sems so/
/amag zor ma'i lo rgyus su/ me Ice 'bar ma'i rgyud sogs
las sangs rgyas 'od srung kyi bstan pa'i mjug tu dpal ldan lha
mo dang bdag cag gi ston pa gnyis smon lam lhan cig tu mdzad
nas de'i skye ba phyi ma la u ma'i sras su 'khrungs pa dang/
abang phyug dang u ma yab yum du gyur pa la brten nas nam mkha'i
gza' skor sogs gsar du byung bar gsungs nas/ de yan chad du
gza' skar sogs med pa Ita bu dang/ u mar 'khrungs pa'i dpal
Idan lha mo'i sku phyi mas bram ze mchog sred dang mnyam (p.
33b) du e ka dza ti bsgrubs par gsungs pas dus Inga phyi'i



Mgon-po
Ma-ning
"dzol che ba dang/ ram sras kyi lo rgyus khungs ma yongs
grags su 'dul ba lung gi lung khungs drangs te sangs rgyas 'od
srung kyi bstan pa'i skabs da Ita'i rgyal po chen po sde bzhi
gnyis nam mkha' iding da ng/ gnyis klur 'khrungs pa dang/ de'i
skye ba phyi ma rgyal po chen po bzhir gyur nas shākya thub
pa'i bstan srung mdzad ces 'od srung kyi gong la da ita'i
rgyal po chen po bzhi med pa lta bu dang/ yang bskal pa thog
ma'i dus nas rgyal po chen po sde bzhis 'jig rten skyong ba
dang/ rdzogs Idan gyi dus su ston pa rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs
pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi dur khrod la phyogs skyong brgyad dang/
sgo bzhir rgyal chen bzhi yod pa du ma gsungs pas 'gal ba itar
snang ba mchis na'ang/ de thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgyu
'phrul gyi bkod pa yin pas 'gal bar mi sems shing skad cig mar
bskal pa dang/ bskal pa skad cig mar bsgyur ba'i bkod pa ston
pas mtha' gcig tu ngos bzung gis tshad gzhal bar aka' ba yin no/
/bstan pa 'di'i mgon po ma hā kā la thams cad kyi khungs
dbang phyug dang/ u ma'i sras ma hā kā la dang/ dpal ldan lha
mo thams cad bu mo tsa muntri la khungs ma brten pa med do/
/mgon po 'di nyid la lha'i dge slong legs ldan nag por
yang grags zhing phyag zhabs kyi lhu tshigs bzhi nas dmag dpon
bzhi po sprul bar gsungs pas so/
/srog bdag 'od kyi rgyal po/ bdud ri nag spungs pa/ klu
bdud nag po srog len/ btsan yam shud amar po mams dang gcig
ste/ rgyal po chen po mam thos sras kyi gyul bzlog chen mo'i
mdos gzhung gi nang tshan mgon po'i sgos mdos las
dur khrod chen po rab 'jigs pa/
/ma la ya zhes grags pa yi/
/1cags mkhar nag po'i nang shed na/
/bdud dang mu stegs bsnol ba'i gdan steng na/
/bskal pa med Itar 'bar ba'i klong dkyil na/
/bdud 'aul lha chen ma hā kā la ni/
/mthing nag mi srun 'jigs byed 'bar ba'i sku/

Mgon-po
Ma-ning
/spyan gsum sdang mig bskal pa'i me ltar 'bar/
/'jigs byed zhal gdangs mche ba mo gtsigs shing/

lag tshom ser po bskal pa'i me Itar 'bar/

/lha min grong khyer sum brtsegs gtan nas bcom/
/lha yi tshogs kyi dgra lhar khyod mchod kyis/
/lha dmag dkar po'i dbugs phyungs nas/

Ma-ning
/legs pa'i rtsal gyi lha min dpung rams bcom/

/tshogs bdag chen po'i dus la bab/ (p. 34a)

nag po mtshan gyi mi 'gyur sku ndog nag/

/nag po dgra la chas pa'i tshe/

/ri rab zon nas thugs la sprug/
1ha min dmag tshogs g.yul ngo zlog/

Connection
with Gñan
Lo-tsā-ba
/bstan srung thams cad kyi rgyal po gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud
dang gdan bzhi dang bde mchog gi bshad rgyud las angos su
bstan pa STOBS 'PHROG NAG PO CHEN PO ZHAL BZHI PA'am SBAS PA'I
MGON PO dang DAM TSHIG GI MGON POr grags pa, 'di ni bcom ldan
'das 'khor lo sdom pa'i thugs ka nas spros te sprul ba dang
zhing skyong dbang phyug chen po'i sras kyi tshul bzung ba'i
bkod pa sogs ji snyed mchis shing/ bla ma gnyan lo tsa ba dar
ma grags zhes bya ba rig pa'i gnas Inga la mkhas shing rdo rje
theg pa dang bstan srung brgya rtsa brgyad kyi bdag por grags
pa bstan srung bran du bkol bar nus pa des rgya gar du byon
te panqi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dang/ ta thā ga tā rakşi ta
la sogs par bla ma mang po bsten/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pa las
chos mang du gsan nas bod du 'byon khar bdag la gsang 'dus
ye shes zhabs lugs kyi dbang rdzogs pa zhig zhu zhes zhus pas/
bla ma'i zhal nas sngon dge bsnyen zhi ba'i go cha Icags kyi
byin pa can zhes bya ba ri po ta lar phyin tel spyan ras gzigs
kha sār pā pi dngos su spyan drangs/ de bi ko ti'i sa phyogs
su bzhugs pas kha sār pā pi'i ri sul du grags/ yul der nga
las byin rlabs che ba'i bla ma 'jan dpal rdo rje'i mal 'byor
ma chen mo skra sen rab tu ring zhing gos dang stan yang skra'i
lwa ba las byed pa zhig bzhugs yod pas/ der (p. 35a) song la
gsol ba thob cig, khyod rang dang 'brel pa yod pas abang dang
gdams ngag mnams gnang bar "dug ces lung bstan/
tshar chen gyis bran rnal 'byor ma gsum yod cing/ dpon
g.yog bzhi po 'di yum bzhi'i mam sprul yin zhes bla ma 'ga'
zhig gsungs zhes bshad/
'phags pa rin po ches chog khrigs mdzad pa'i dngul bre
ma las shing sdong gcig gi khog pa na doon goyog Inga brda
skad gsungs/ goyog no gsum gyis re mos bgyis te grong na
'tsho ba 'tshol zhing sgrub pa mdzad cing 'dug/ mandal phul

pa
nas dbang bskur zhu byas pas khyod la sus bstan gsungs/ ngas

gsungs nas/ de bzhin du bgyi'o zhus pas 'o na mtha' 'khob kyi
mi yin pas/ mi ma yin dang/ gcan gzan dang/ sbrul la sogs pa'i

lon tsa na/ da ngas lha las gnang ba thob pas dbang bskur bya
yis tshogs dang yo byad 'tshol zhig gsungs nas gser zho gsum

gang la sha byas/ zho gang la zan dang spos la sogs pa byas

drongs gsungs/

received by
Gnyan
ngas mgron mi mnyed byas pas/ 'o na sngar gyi grogs po
de bos dang gsungs nas/ bos pas mi rkang phyungs nas bus pas

mnyes nas dbang yongs su rdzogs par gnang ngo/

ba 'dus pa'i nan ngag/ ugni şa/ sgrol ma/ chos skyong 'di
dngos su gnang ste/ dbang dus su bram ze de la khyod kyis 'di'i

ba'i thugs la rgya gar gyi grub thob mams kyi slob ma lo tsā

pa

da. Ita'i bar du kha'u'i brag rdzong gi gnas su tsa turmu kha

Nag-po

Mgon-po
be'u-bum
dpal ldan sa skya pa mnams kyi thun ong ma yin pa'i srung
ma'i gtso bor bzhugs shing gur mgon la mgon po che ba dang/
'di la chung ba zhes 'bod cing/ snyan pa'i grags pas khyab/
dus phyis thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'aun rgya mtsho nas
bzung ste kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i dbang po rim byon gyi chos
srung gi gtso bor mdzad/ de dag las rin par brgyud te chos
rgyal gter bdag gling pas bdag cag gi mam 'dren bla ma dam
pa gar dbang dharma'i mtshan can la zhal bsñen dus dang agrub
dus kyi rjes gnang gnyis dang be bum yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung
bstsal zhing/ rje bla ma mchog gis de dag dang bram nag bshan
pa drug skor la sogs pa'i man ngag mnams kho bo la dgyes bzhin
du bstsal lo/
mgon po 'di la spyir mam 'gyur mtha' yas pa mchis kyang/

Bstan srung
/gsang sngags srung mar dbang yang bskur/
Rematı
/mtshan yang sngags srung nag mo bya/
/thams cad gsod pa'i las byed ma/
/srin mo ral goig sha za ma/
/rnal 'byor yongs kyi grogs byed pas/
/mtshan yang dgra 'dul nad 'tshong ma/
/de nas tsha ba'i nad gtong ba/
/mtshan yang bal (zhang blon gyi yum de yin no) mo kun gdug ma/
/khrag rims yams nad gtong byed pas/
/mtshan yang nag mo khrag 'dzag ma/
/ltag ngan cho 'phrul gtong byed pas/
/mtshan yang mon mo nag mo byas/ /zhes mtshan gyi mam grangs
kyang brjod kyi mi longs bsam yas te/
phyag na rdo rje sprul pa'i skus/
/nyid kyis sprul pa bstan par bsam/ /zhes gsungs/ de lta
bu'i dpal ldan lha mo sngags kyi srung ma des rang bzhin lhun
grub kyi gzhal yas khang chen por bzhugs pa'i skabs su rang gi
sprul pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje bde byed mas bskul te khros ma
gsang rgyud la sogs pa gsungs pa yin te/ khros ma nag mo'i gsang
rgyud las/
dpal rang byung gi royal mo la phyag 'tshal 10/ /'ai skad
bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na:
dpal ldan rang byung rgyal mo'i gnas:
rang bzhin lhun gyis rdzogs pa yi:
bhandha 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang:
dkar dang ser dang dmar nag pa'i:
'phrin las rnam bzhi lhun gyis grub:
zhi bas spa bkong rgyas pas zil gnon la:
dbang gis dbang sdud drag pos sgrol bar byed:
khams gsum abang sdud drag po'i gzhal yas ni:



Remati
dri za la sogs phyogs skyong bcu yi mgos:
shar la sogs pa de bzhin rab tu mdzes:
bhanda'i gzhal yas lhun gyis grub pa las:
gnam 1cags 'bar ba'i gzer chen rab tu btab:
ye shes Inga ldan kha dog rab tu 'phro:
lha brgyad ka ba klu brgyad gdung du bres:
gza' brgyad (p. 43b) khyams bres rgyu skar gral lcam gyis:
ru tra dkar po ser po dmar po dang:
1jang gu la sogs sa yi thog kyang phub:
ye shes bzhi ldan sgo bzhir gnas pa ni:
sgo skyes g.yas g•yon chu srin 'gran pa la:
bzas pa pho mo'i ya them ma them byas:
chu srin thod pa'i rta babs rab tu mdzes:
bhandha sum cu rtsa gnyis rab tu gtibs:
chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu nyams ni dga':
'od zer dmar nag 'phro 'du rgyun mi chad:
chos kyi 'khor lo smug nag gdugs phub nas:
g.yas g•yon chu srin phrug gu blta zhing 'phyo:
seng ge stag dang chu srin dom gyi mgos:
bhandha 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang bgyis te:
thod pa'i drwa ba tshil bu'i drwa phyed pa:
zhe sdang sbrul nag chun po'i thag pas brgyus:
gser gyi dril 'khrol rin chen 'od zer 'bar:
sbrul nag gdug pa'i chun po nyi li li:
thabs dang shes rab nyi zla gsal rgyas te:
gzhal yas phyi nang med par 'od gsal 'bar:
thod pa khrag 'dzag dar bu khad du ldan:
sprul pa'i lha mos 'dod yon mchod pa stob:
rgyal mtshan chen po bzhi yang gnas pa yi:
byang shar sprul pa rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan dang:
shar lho 'dul byed lcags kyi rgyal mtshan dang:



Bstan srung
of
Doogee
93
Remati
the
lho nub lha srin dar gyi rgyal mtshan dang:
mub byang dmar nag khrag gi rgyal mtshan dang:
rgyal mtshan chen po bzhi yang de bzhin gnas:
de ltar gnas pa'i gzhal yas chen po de:
dpal ldan rang byung rgyal mo bzhugs pa'i gnas:
gzhal yas nang rim khrag gi rgya mtshor gnas:
sprul pa'i ma mo mkha' 'gro bzhugs pa'i gnas:
phyi rim thod pa lcags kyi grong khyer ni:
bdud dang srin po gshin rje bzhugs pa'i gnas:
tha ma lcags ri nag pos bskor ba'i nang:
dur khrod chen po brgyad kyis bskor ba'o:
dur khrod nag po phyogs skyong mgo bo dang:
ro ni sna tshogs man par bam pa dang:
rus dang mags dang rnam par bam pa dang:
stag dang gzig dang gcan gzan sna tshogs dang:
dur bya kangka 'dab chags sna tshogs dang:
shing dang chu la sogs pa'ang de bzhin gnas:
sha za khrag 'thung las kyi mkha' 'gro dang:
ging dang langka gnod sbyin pho mo'i gnas:
gzhan yang dur khrod ma mo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs:
dpal chen bka' la gtogs pa bsam mi khyab:
de dag thams cad 'khor dang thabs cig bzhugs:
dur khrod gzhal yas de yi phyi rim na:
dur khrod me dpung 'bar bas bskor te gnas:
chos nyid klong du mi 'syur mi shigs rtags:
rdo rje'i ra ba yongs su rgya ma chad:
de lta bu yi gzhal yas 'bar ba de:
'phrin las ram bzhi lhun gyis grub pa'i gnas:
pho brang gru gsum mkha' dbyings bde chen na:
dur khrod ro yi gdan la 'gying ba'i tshul:



Remati
bud med nag mo mdzes pa'i cha byad can:
dkar mo nag mo ser mo dmar mo'i tshogs:
nyid las mi gzhan 'khor gyis bskor te gnas:
nyid kyi the tshon rgyas par bcad pa'i phyir:
phyag rdor sprul pa lha mo bde byed ma:
nyid las mi gzhan dmod pa'i mtshon cha can:
rang las sprul pa'i nag mo 'bum dang bcas:
rang byung rgyal mo nyid la 'di skad gsol:
e ma ho: rang byung rgyal mo nyid:
bdag ni rtag tu khyod la 'dud:
khyod kyis byin rlabs thugs rje gang:
rgya cher bdag la bshad du gsol: zhes gsol pas: de'i dus
de'i tshe: dpal rang byung gi rgyal mo zhes bya ba yang sku
mthing nag 'bar ba la mche ba gtsigs pa: ral pas sa gzhi khebs
pa la: spyi bo'i gtsug na g.yu yi ral pa mthing ga 'bar ba
gcig gnas pa: zhabs gyad kyi dor stabs su bzhugs pa: g.yas na
bam chen po'i tsitta srog rtsa dang bcas nas bzung ba: (p. 44a)
gyon na g.yu'i spyang mo bkye nas khra thabs su bsnams pa ste:
ti ra dang ro yi gdan la: trag raksha zhes bya ha'i sngags
brjod nas: nyid kyi sku las sprul pa'i ma no bkye ste: sku'i
sprul pa las bal mo nag mo dang: gsung gi sprul pa las ma mo
srin mo'i tshogs dang: thugs kyi sprul pa la mon mo'i tshogs
dang: gzhan yang sbyor ging dang: sgrol ging la sogs pa khram
thogs kyi bdud dang: srog good kyi ging po dang bcas te sprul
pa mang po nyid las bkye bas: snang srid thams cad dus gcig
la goyos par gyur to:
nad kyi rlangs pa dang: mtshon gyi bskal ba dang: bskal
pa phra mo dang: dug sbal yams nad dang: gnam lcags ser ba la
sogs pa dus gcig 'khrugs par syur te: slar yang bdud pho mo
de dag rang la rdzogs par gyur te: snang srid thams cad dus
gcig tu bde ba la bkod do:
dug sbal dang yams nad la sogs pa kun kyang bdud rtsi



Bstan srung
94
chen por gyur te: thams cad thugs rje chen po'i bde ba la bkod
Remati
do: khros nag gsang ba'i rgpud las gleng gzhi'i skabs te dang
po'o: zhes gsungs/
mdor bsdu na/ dmag gi rgyal mo lnga/ ye shes kyi rje mo
bcu bzhi/ sman mo lnga bcu rtsa brgyad la sogs pa srid pa ma
mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo thams cad rang byung rgyal mo
dam sngags kyi srung ma i ka dza ti'am e ka tsa ti rang gi mnam
'phrul 'ba' zhig ste khros na gsang rgyud las/
rang byung rgyal mos 'di skad ces gsungs so/
/nga ni dus gsum thams cad du/
Inga yi thugs rje rgyun mi chad/
/nga ni bde gshegs sbyor sde mo/
/nga ni mal 'byor sbyor sde mo/
/nga ni mal 'byor bsgrub sde mo/
/dam tshig can gyi dgra lha mo/
/dam tshig nyams pa'i srog good ma/
/nga ni rang byung rgyal mo ste/
/nga ni nga las byung ba yin/
/thams cad nga yi sprul pa yin/
/dkar mo sku yi sprul pa yin/
/smug mo gsung gi sprul pa yin/
/nag mo thugs kyi sprul pa yin/
/ser mo yon tan sprul pa yin/
/dmar mo 'phrin las sprul pa yin/
de dag thams cad nga yin pas/
/nga yi sprul pa bsam mi khyab/
/nga yi ming ni cir yang grags/
Inga ni 'phrin las thams cad byed:
Akun gyis 'phrin las 'chol 'dod na/
/thams cad nga yin nga la Itos/
/nga nyid yongs su bzung bar gyis/ /zhes gsungs/



Remati
very inter-
esting!
khros na nag mo gsang ba snying gi rgyud las/
khros ma nag mos 'jig rten gyi mes po shrī ral pa can
tshangs pa gdong bzhi par sprul te rtsa zhal las bram ze'i ston
pa tshangs pa byung ste bdag rtag pa'i chos ston/ g.yon zhal
nas e ra'i ston pa khyab 'jug byung nas bdag khyab pa'i chos
bstan/ rgyab zhal nas legs ldan gyi fan bu dbang phyug chen
po byung nas bdag bde ba'i chos bstan/ g.yas zhal las grangs
can gyi ston pa 'jigs byed byung nas bdag gtsang ba'i chos
bstan/ sku gsung thugs las sprul pa'i khro bo nyi khri chig
stong sprul nas ngan sngags kyi rgyud mnams gsungs par bshad/
lha mo rdo rie nag mo dbang phyug ma'i rgyud las/
gong du bshad pa Itar gyi lha dang lha ma yin g.yul bkye
ba'i gleng gzhi la brten nas/ lha ma yin mams btul ba dang/
rgyal chen bzhi/ lha ma yin gyi rgyal po he ra ni ke'u shu/
de'i chung ma phag sna ma klu rigs bzhi la sogs pa btul ba'i
tshul rgyas par gsungs/

bcom idan 'das kyis dpal ldan lha mo sgrol ging du dbang
bskur/ drag po 'dul ba'i nus pa dang ldan par bya phyir zhing
chen gyi g.yang gzhi'i dbang bskur/ bdud dang srin po las
rgyal bar bya phyir/ g.yul du bsad pa'i mgo 'phreng dang/ thams
cad bsad cing bsgral kyang/ bag chags kyis mi gos par bya ba'i
phyir/ re ide nag po'i gos dang/ sman mo mnams zil gyis (p.
44b) gnod pa'i phyir snyan g.yas sengge dang/ klu gnad la dbab

sems can gyi tshe srog la dbang bsgyur ba'i phyir du rtse gsum
dang nad rkyal/ 'jig rten la dbang bsgyur ba'i phyir du thod
khrag/ dan tshig la bya ra mdzad pa'i phyir du 'phrul gyi me
long/ mkha' 'gro rnams dam la bsdu ba'i phyir du gser gyi mge'u

Rematı
de'i tshe brgya byin la sogs pa'i 'khor thams cad rab tu
skrags te/ brgya byin gyis rdo rje/ tshangs pas rma bya'i
rgyal mtshan/ khyab 'jug gis nyi zla'i rgyal mtshan/ ram sras
kyis seng ge'i rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' lha bran gyis dril bu/
klu'i rgyal po mnams kyi sbrul gyi gdengs ka/ sa bdag pa las
stag gi rgyal mtshan/ srin po dang sha za mams kyis thod pa'i
'phreng ba dang zhag gi sor ris/ dpal nag po chen pos mdung
thung/ 'khor gzhan rnams kyis rang rang gi yo byad dang/ lag
cha phul te mngon par bstod pas srid pa gsum na 'gran zla dang
bral ba'i mthu rtsal can du gyur par gsungs/
ma mo 'bum rgyud las/ dpal chen po mngon rdzogs rgyal
po'i thugs kyi rtsa bzhi las/ sha dar (?read: shar) dkar gyi
skud pa nas srid pa'i ma mo sku mdog dkar mo g.yas na snying
khrag dang/ g.yon na mda' gzhu thogs pa nyi ma 'bum dang zla
ba stong gis brgyan pa sprul te srin mo dkar mo dung lo can
zhes bya bar grags/ nyi zla thod 'phreng can nam/ nyi zla
stong phreng can yang 'di nyid do/
lho baidūr.ya 'dra ba'i rtsa sgo nas srid pa'i ma mo

dang/ g.yon 'phrul gyi me long bsnams pa rma bya'i thul pa
gsol ba/

mo zangs kyi drel rta smug po bzhon pa/ phyag ntshan dung gi
ga'u bsnams pa dang/

triluba

Remati
ma mo khyod du sprul par mdzad:
yang dag nyid du rgyal kun yum:
rnam pa rag gdong khro mo'i gzugs: zhes rgyal ba thams
cad kyi yum kun tu bzang mo nyid yin par gsungs so:
mdor na snang srid 'khor 'das kyis bsdus pa'i chos thams
cad rang rig byang chub sems kyi ngo bor rdzogs pa te/ gang
snang gi snang ba thams cad rang sems las logs su med cing/
rang sems kyi ngo bo rdo rje gsum gyi bdag nyid la/ ye nas
Thun rdzogs su mchis pas de'i phyir na de Itar yin pa la yin
par ngo shes pa'i sgo nas rig stong khyab gdal chen por mnyam
par 'jog pa ni ma mo'i lta ba/ rang rig pa'i ye shes kyi rtsal
snang spyad bya spyod byed dang bral ba'i ngang du/ snang ba
sku/ grags pa gsung/ dran rig thugs su rgyas 'debs shing rig
pa'i sgo nas 'phrin las mam pa bzhi'i skabs dang ntshangs
par spyod pa ni ma mo'i spyod pa/ gang snang gi snang ba'i
ngo bo spros pa dang bral ba ma mo'i chos nyid du lhun gyis
grub pas gdod nas ye sangs rgyas pa dang/ thams cad kyang thabs
shes gnyis su med pa'i bdag nyid de snang stong zung 'jug gi
rang bzhin du rdzogs pa la gsal 'grib med par 'jog pa ma mo'i
bsgom pa/ de Itar rig pa'i sgo nas snang srid ma mo'i dkyil
'khor du bsgrub pa ni ma mo'i sgrub pa/ rang rig dang ye shes
sems dang sems nyid/ thabs dang shes rab/ sangs rgyas dang
sems can/ 'khor ba dang myang 'das/ phyi nang dang snod bcud/
yul dang dbang po thams cad gnyis med du sbyor ba ni ma mo'i
sbyor ba/ khams gsum rang sems su shes pas srid gsum rdo rje
gsum dang/ 'khor ba myang 'das snang srid thams cad ma mo'i
rang bzhin du sgrol ba ni ma mo'i sgrol ba/ sems can thams cad
chos dbyings su gso ba/ phyi nang snod bcud byang chub kyi

Rematı
shes Inga dang/ dug gsum sku gsung thugs sogs su bsad/ de
snang srid thams cad bsad bya gsod byed dang bral ba'i ngang
du bsad pa ni ma mo'i bsad pa del
gsang rgyud las/
snang srid 'di Itar snang ba'i chos:
phyi nang snod bcud thams cad kun:
ma mo nyid las gzhan ma yin:
ma ni kun gzhi dbyings kyi klong:
mo ni byang sems ye shes dang:
dbyings dang ye shes don rtogs pa:
ma dang mo yi don rtogs yin:
ma mo de ltar rtogs pa ni:
rtogs pa mngon gyur Ita ba yin:
de Itar gnyis med don rtogs na:
bgrod pa med pa'i sa chen non:
yang na ma mo'i lta ba ni:
be hones
ma mo snying po byang chub sems:
snying po nyid las gzhan ma yin:
snying po byang chub ye sangs rgyas:
thams cad dag pas sangs rgyas yin:
lhun gyis grub pas ma mo yin:
gnyis su med pas ma mo yin:
rang las byung bas ma mo yin:
yongs la khyab pas ma mo yin:
cir yang snang bas ma mo yin:
Eang yang 'char bas ma mo yin:
khyab par gdal bas ma mo yin:
mi 'gyur mi shigs ma mo yin:
gcig las med pas ma mo yin:
tha dad snang bas ma mo yin:
ma mo bsgrub cing sgrub tu med:

pe
97
Remati
ma mo bsgoms shing bsgrubs na 'grub:
bgrod du med pas gar yang phyin:
btsal du med des gar yang 'grub:
'dogs su med pas thams cad yin:
tha dad snang ba gnyis su med:
gnyis med don rtogs ma mo yin:
ma ni snying po byang chub sems:
mo ni rang byung ye shes yin:
snying po byang chub sems las ni:
ma mo gzhan las brtsal ni mnyed:
rang byung ye shes de bzhin nyid:
ye nas (p. 45b) lhun gyis rdzogs par gnas:
khyung chen nam mkhar Iding ba'ang:
snang srid phyi rgya riabs kyis chod:
snying po byang chub nyid las ni:
ma mo zhes ni gdags su med:
snying po byang chub sems las ni:
ma mo gzhan nas btsal mi mnyed:
sems las kun byung thams cad sems :
ma mo byang chub sems kyis brgyan:
de Itar gnyis med rtogs pa na:
ma mo bsgon zhing bsgrub mi dgos:
ma mo lus dang grib ma 'dra: zhes gsungs so:
khros ma'i gsang rgyud las:
Ita ba bstan pa'i skabs te gnyis pa'o:
de nas spyod pa bka' stsal pa:
gzugs su snang ba thams cad kun:
ma mo'i sku yi bdag nyid yin:
sgra ru grags pa thams cad kun:
ma mo'i gsung gi bdag nyid yin:



Remati
sems kyi dran rtog thams cad kun:
ma mo'i thugs kyi bdag nyid yin:
rang byung ye shes thams cad kun:
ma mo'i yon tan bdag nyid yin:
thams cad rang las byung bas na:
it ang totoo
'phrin las mam bzhi ci spyad kyang:

de Itar spyad lugs ci spyad kyang:

spyod pa bstan pa'i skabs te gsum pa'o: zhes pa dang/

Remati
shes rab ting 'dzin gnyis med na:
de yang ma mo bsgom pa yin:
lta ba spyod pa gnyis med na:
de yang ma mo bsgom pa yin:
phyi snod nang bcud gnyis med na:
de yang ma mo bsgom pa yin:
yul dang dbang po gnyis med na:
de yang ma mo bsgom pa yin:
ma mo sems su gnyis med na:
bsgom pa med pa'i bsgom pa yin: zhes gsungs so:
khros ma nag mo'i gsang ba'i rgyud las:
bsgom pa bstan pa'i skabs ste bzhi pa'o:
de nas ma mo bsgrub pa ni:
snang zhing srid pa'i chos mams kun:
thams cad ma mor bsgrub par bya:
ma mor rang byung sems su bsgrub:
sems nyid ye sgrub chen po ste:
snang med kun tu snang ba'i gdos pa can:
bya ba byed cing ntshan nyid ci dgar 'gyur:
nor bu rin chen Ita bu'i sems nyid de:
ma mo 'gro ba sems can yongs la 'phro:
de nyid ma spangs ma mo'i sgrub pa yin: zhes gsungs so/
khros ma nag mo'i rgyud las/
sgrub pa bstan pa'i skabs te inga pa'o:
lha mo bde byed yang gsol pa:

sgom sgrub gnyis ni bdag go na:
nyid kyi sbyor sgrol ji ltar lags :
rang byung rgyal mos bshad du gsol:
de skad gsol pa gsan nas kyang:



Remati
rang byung rgyal mos bka' stsal pa:
bde gshegs thugs kyi ye shes las:
rang rig ye shes blo yis sbyar:
thams cad chos kyi chos nyid las:
sems kyi sems nyid gnyis med sbyor:
thabs dang shes rab gnyis med sbyor:
sangs rgyas sems can gnyis med sbyor:
'khor ba myang "das gnyis med sbyor:
phyi nang snod bcud gnyis med sbyor:
yul dang dbang po gnyis med sbyor:
snang srid thams cad ma mor sbyor:
ma mo snying po'i sems su sbyor:
sems nyid ye sbyor chen po yin: (p. 46a)
de Bueu
de Itar gnyis med sbyor ba na:
de ni ma mo'i sbyor ba yin: zhes gsungs so:
khros ma nag mo'i gsang rgyud las:
sbyor ba bstan pa'i skabs te drug pa'o:
de nas sgrol ba bstan pa ni:
khams gsum thams cad rang gi sems yin pas:
ye sangs rgyas pa'i khams gsum yongs su sgrol:
snang srid thams cad rang gi sems yin pas:
ye sangs rgyas pas bya byed 'bad rtsol bral:
srid gsum dag pa'i zhing du ye grol yin:
sems can rgyud drug phung por snang ba yang:
rang gi sems nyid yin te ye sangs rgyas:
rgyud drug rtsad bcad dag pa'i zhing du sgrol:
rgyu Inga las kyi sgo yang rang gi sems:
sems nyid sangs rgyas ngan song lam yang med:
ye nas dag pas dag pa'i zhing du sgrol:
snang srid thams cad ma mo'i ngang du bsgral:
ma mo mkha' 'gro'i byang chub sems su bsgral:
sems nyid sangs rgyas ye grol chen po yin: zhes gsungs so:

Remati
khros ma nag mo'i rgyud las:
sgrol ba bstan pa'i skabs te bdun pa'o:
lha mo bde byed yang gsol pa:
sbyor sgrol gnyis ni bdag go na:
nyid kyi gso bsad ji ltar lags:
sbyor sgrol bdag mos bshad du gsol:
de skad gsol ba gsan nas kyang:
rang byung rgyal mos bka' stsal pa:
'khor ba'i sems can thams cad kun:
bde chen chos kyi dbyings su gso:
phyi nang snod bcud thams cad kun:
snying po byang chub sems su gso:
thugs rje chen po'i byin brlabs kyis:
khams gsum sems can nyon mongs gso:
'du ba'i nad kyis zin pa rnams:
bdud rtsi chen po'i sman gyis gso:
thugs rje'i rgyun thag chad pa rams:
rang byung ye shes thugs rjes gso:
dam tshig rgyun thag chad pa mams:
mi brjed gzungs kyi thugs rjes gso:
shes rab mi rtag shi ba mams:
ting 'dzin ma yengs brtan pos gso:
shes rab me lce chad pa rams:
rtogs pa khyad par brtan pos gso:
rang byung ye shes rgyun chad pa:
snying po byang chub sems su gso:
sems kyi de nyid ma rtogs pa:
shes rab ting 'dzin brtan pos gso:
ma mo mkha' 'gro'i gdug gtum pa:
snying po byang chub sems su gso: zhes gsungs so:



Remati
khros ma nag mo'i rgyud las:
gso ba bstan pa'i skabs te brgyad pa'o:
bsad pa'i sbyor ba bstan pa ni:
dug Inga ye shes Inga ru bsad:
dug gsum sku gsung thugs su bsad:
sdug bsngal bde ba chen por bsad:
'khor ba myang ngan 'das par bsad:
shes rab me lce 'bar ba yis:
gzung 'dzin rlung dmar 'khrug pa bsad:
shes rab me stag chen po yis:
mam rtog gru char 'bab pa bsad:
man par rtogs pa'i khyad par gyis:
ma rtogs rmongs pa'i gti mug bsad:
ye shes nyi ma 'od gsal bas:
gti mug mun pa 'thibs pa bsad:
snang srid chos mams sems su bsad:
ma mo mkha' 'gro'i dbyings su bsad:
shi ba med pa ye bsad yin:
sems can thams cad sems su bsad:
rtogs pa mngon du gyur pa dang:
ting 'dzin las su rung ba na:
snang srid thams cad bsad par bya:

sras
/'gro ba'i bsam pa yongs rdzogs mdzad/

/gangga'i bye ma'i grangs snyed kyi/
/rgyal mchog mnams kyis rab gsungs pa'i/
/' od zer rgyas pa zhes bya ba'i/
/zhing na sangs rgyas nyi ma'i zhal/
/chos bstan pa na bdag gis kyang/
/der ni rang gis dngos thos te/

/de dag bdag gi rab bshad kyis/
/sems can kun don gces pa'o/
khyod ni rab tu mnyam bzhag nyon/

dus na/ 'od zer mam par rgyas pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi
khams su/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas nyi ma'i snying po bkod pa'i zhal zhes bya
ba 'jig rten du byung bar gyur te/ de'i 'khor yang tshad med
cing grangs med do/
/age slong gi dge 'dun yang grangs med cing gzhan las 'das
so/ /de'i chos kyang bskal pa 'bum drug khri'i bar du gnas so/

to/ /de'i tshe de'i dus na/ nga yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
rgyas nyi ma'i snying po'i zhabs 'bring byed pa'i dus na byang

tshogs kyis spras pa/ rgyan du ma sna tshogs kyis mdzes para

/pho log hur thum dgra la thongs/

/chibsu dmar po glog 'gyu bcibs/
78.yas na bse mdung mo dbal bsnams/
/gri 'thab drag po agra la thong/ /zhes bskul 10/
/yon tan rin chen "byung ba'i rgyud las/
phyi Itar bskul ba'i le'u ste dgu pa', zhes nang 'khor
sprul pa'i ging (p. 75b) bzhi bskul bar gsungs pa'i shar ging
tshangs pa dung thod can ni be har 'di nyid yin la/ de bzhin
du lho ging rdor legs/ nub ging bdud mgon/ byang ging yam shud
dmar po mams srung ma'i gtso bor bsten mi rung bar thal ba
dang/ mam sras chos skyong du bsten/ sprul 'khor de dag bzhag
pa'i dbye ba 'byed dgos par 'gyur bas legs par brtags na nges
pa myed par 'gyur ro/
/gzhan yang khram thogs nag po'i rgyud kyi le'i so bzhi
par gshin rje gshed kyi dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs bskul ba'i
skabs su bdud yab rje nag po/ bdud mo re ma tī/ legs ldanag po!
rdo rje legs pa/ yam shud dmar po/ yulha phywa sang/ gnam thelu
dkar po sogs thun mong ma yin pa'i 'khor mams bskul tshul
gsungs pa te/ de nyid las/
hūm dur khrod "bar ba'i dkyil 'khor 'dir/
/bstan pa srung ba'i dregs pa brgyad/
/phyogs bzhi mtshams brgyad dbang byed pa/

/nyi zla gza' skar sprul pa phyogs bcur 'gyed/

78.yas pas khram shing goyon pas dgra stwa 'dzin/
/'chi bdag bdud po khyod kyi dus la bab/
/byang shar mtshams la dbang byed bdud mo kun gyi gtso/
/lha mo nag mo 'jigs pa'i gzugs byad can/
/bka' bzlog nag mo bdud kyi yum gcig ma/
/gcer bu dre'u zhon tshangs bdud gshin rje'i lcam/
/khram bam g.yas pa nad kyi rkyal pa g.yon/
/nag mo dre'u (or: re'u) zhon khyod kyi dus la bab/
/shar lho mtshams su dbang mdzad ngon nag ni/
/sku la ljang nag ber chen gsol/
/phyag na mda' gzhu dgra snying 'bigs/
/ral pa nag po mun rum 'dra/
/sma ra ag tshom me itar 'bar/
/' breng zhags nag po se ral kha/
/bdud rta bra nag chibsu bcibs/
/sprul pa mon nag mang po 'gyed/
/bdua ngon nag po'i dus la babs/
/lho nub mtshams la dbang mdzad pa/
/sku lus gcig tu ma nges X 'khor ni thelu rang stong/
/'jig rten 'di na mthu rtsal rab tu 'phags/
/gdod nas ma skyes rang bzhin dag pa'i sku/
/rdo rje legs pa sku la bse khrab gsol/
/phyag na shel mdung ba dan rtse inga bsnams/
/chibsu ngang pa gser sgang chibs/
/mnyam nyid rig pa'i skyes bu'i dus la babs/
/hum dgung sngon mthon po'i dkyil 'khor yangs pa na/
/shel ndung dkar po dar dkar btags pa bsnams/

/rta dkar zangs dmar chibsu bcibs/
/myur ngyogs chen po'i dus la babs/
/byang phyogs yam shud dmar po ni/
/btsan rgod dmar po srog gi bdud/
/sku la dar dmar zab slog gsol/
/abu la zangs kyi rmog zhu mnabs/
/zangs zhags g.yas la ral gri g.yon/
/chibsu zangs rta amar po bcibs/
/sgrol ging bshan pa'i dus la babs/
/phyogs bzhi dag la mnga' mdzad cing/
/yul chen mams kyi dmag dpon mdzad/
/sku stod zhing chen &•yang gzhi gsol/
/sku smad stag gi sham thabs can/
/chibsu phya rgyal dmigs pa bcibs/
/sog le g.yas la nad rkyal &.yon/
/yulha phya sangs dus la babs/
/nam mkha' stong la dbang bsgyur cing/
/cho 'phrul dpag tu med pa yi/
/srog abang 'gugs la (p. 76a) la mnga' mdzad pa/
/chu gri g.yas la zhags pa s•yon/
/gnam thel dkar po'i dus la babs/ /zhes pas bskul bar
bya'o/ zhes bshad pas/ gnam thel dkar po ni be har dang gcig
la gshin rje gshed kyi dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs su bzhugs
na gtso kkchor dgongs pa mnyan par 'gyur zhing/ rig 'dzin gyi
sa la bzhugs par zhal gyis bzhes dgos pas/ be har dang mam
sras la mchog dman gyi zhal blang 'dzin pa gnang na zhabs
'dren dus gcig tu 'chor ba ma gtogs thabs med do/
/de Ita bu'i rgyal po chen po 'di la/ gar mkhan mchog gi
rtogs pa le'u bcu gsun pa dang/ sna tshogs grub pa'i rgyud
dang/ bai shra wa na khram thogs kyi rgyud dang/ dbyug pa can
gyi rgyud dang/ yon tan rin po che 'byung ba'i rgyud dang/
dmag dpon chen po'i rgyud dang/ gnod sbyin syi rgyud le'u bcu



Bstan srung

sras
dgu pa la sogs pa'i bod du 'gyur ba brgya dang dgu mchis/ Rnam-thos-
spyir ni nor gyi bdag pos gsungs pa stong phrag sum cu/
yab drang srong mam mang thos pas gsungs pa 'bum phrag gcig
la sogs pa yod par grags/
khram thogs nag po'i rgyud tshad ldan min par bzhed pa'i
mkhas pa chen po dag kyang snang/ gsang sngags gsar rying/
bka' gter mdo rgyud thams cad nas gsungs shing/ sngon byon
gyi mkhas grub phal mo ches chos skyong gis gtso bor mdzad/
khyad par zangs dkar lo tsā ba la chos skyong 'di nyid kyi
bka' babs shin tu che bas/ chos rgyun phal cher de nyid nas
mched pa la/ dus phyis rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan
gyi gsung sras sa skya pa mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags
kyis rgyal po chen po 'di'i bka' mi 'dra ba bco Inga'i rjes
gnang gi yi ge nor 'dzin dpal mo'i rayan 'phreng zhes bya ba.
mdzad/
kho bo cag gis kyang yi ge de nyid kyi steng nas dang
po'i sangs rgyas gar dbang dharmā'i mtshan can gyi spyan sngar
rgyal po 'di'i chos skor mams zhal shes dang bcas legs par
thob pa yin no/
/mam sras phyi sgrub sprin gseb ma/ nang sgrub mdung
dmar can/ gsang sgrub rta sngon ma/ yang gsang phyag mtshan
bzhi pa mams ni chos rgyal gter bdag gling pa nas brgyud de
rdo rje 'dzin pa che mchog 'dus pa rtsal gyi spyan sngar thob/
deng sang ni zhwa ser cod pan 'chang ba'i ring lugs 'dzin
pa mams kyis srung ma'i gtso bor mdzad cing grags che mod/
'on kyang lo rgyus kyi nges pa 'di dag tshul bzhin du myed
pa nyin mo'i skar ma tsam du zad pas 'dir khungs ldan gyi
gzhung las btus te legs par bkod pa yin no/
/ra shag gi gter byon man sras kyi gsol khar rgyal gsol
'phrin las don bcu ma rang gi tshig bcos med du byung/ mam

lo tsā bas/
